       <article about="/grammys" class="node node--main node--full node--main--full" data-id="22" data-title="The GRAMMYs" data-type="main" data-url="/grammys" id="node-main-22" role="article" search_type="" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">
        <header>
         <span class="rdf-meta element-hidden" content="The GRAMMYs" property="dc:title">
         </span>
        </header>
        <div class="node__content">
         <div class="field field--name-title-field field--type-text field--label-hidden">
          <div class="field__items">
           <div class="field__item even">
            <h1 class="hide-h1-on-front-page">
             The GRAMMYs
            </h1>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="field field--name-field-rocks-and-streams field--type-entityreference field--label-hidden">
          <div class="field__items">
           <div class="field__item even">
            <article about="/admin/tra/rocks-and-streams/manage/rocks_and_streams_for_22" class="entity entity-rocks-and-streams rocks-and-streams-rocks-and-streams" typeof="">
             <div>
              <div class="rocks-and-stream-wrapper default-layout">
               <div class="stream">

  // getting value of cookie 'USERCONSENT'
function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
    for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
      var c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
        c = c.substring(1);
      }
      if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
      }
    }
    return "";
  }
